### Write - 2026-03-13 07:09:35 UTC [08:09:35 CEST]

**User Request:** cancelled the WF (it was frozen) - do the tests as suggested, so you finally see that completed steps are not turning green and that the step-into / step button leads to state jumps

**Tool:** Write
**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>dashboard/workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * Playwright E2E tests for UKB Workflow Graph node coloring.\n *\n * Validates that:\n * 1. Completed steps turn green (fill #166534, stroke #15803d)\n * 2. Running steps show green with bold stroke (strokeWidth 4)\n * 3. Pending steps stay grey (fill #f9fafb)\n * 4. Sub-step arcs show correct colors\n * 5. \"Data Preparation\" label appears (not \"Batch\")\n * 6. Step advancement doesn't cause state jumps\n *\n * These tests write workflow-progress.json directly and let the dashboard\n * poll it via its /api/ukb/processes endpoint.\n */\n\nimport { test, expect, type Page } from '@playwright/test'\nimport { writeFileSync, existsSync, readFileSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs'\nimport { join } from 'path'\n\nconst CODING_ROOT = join(__dirname, '..', '..', '..')\nconst PROGRESS_FILE = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data', 'workflow-progress.json')\nconst DASHBOARD_URL = 'http://localhost:3032'\n\n// Expected color constants from ukb-workflow-graph.tsx\nconst COLORS = {\n  completed: { fill: '#166534', stroke: '#15803d', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  running:   { fill: '#166534', stroke: '#22c55e', strokeWidth: '4' },\n  paused:    { fill: '#92400e', stroke: '#f59e0b', strokeWidth: '4' },\n  pending:   { fill: '#f9fafb', stroke: '#d1d5db', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  failed:    { fill: '#fee2e2', stroke: '#ef4444', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  // Status indicator circle colors\n  statusIndicator: {\n    completed: '#22c55e',\n    running: '#3b82f6',\n    failed: '#ef4444',\n    pending: '#d1d5db',\n  },\n  // Sub-step arc colors\n  substep: {\n    completed: { fill: '#22c55e', stroke: '#16a34a' },\n    running:   { fill: '#3b82f6', stroke: '#2563eb' },\n    pending:   { fill: '#e5e7eb', stroke: '#9ca3af' },\n  },\n}\n\n// Saved progress to restore after tests\nlet savedProgress: string | null = null\n\n/**\n * Build a state-machine-format workflow-progress.json.\n * The server.js bridgeStateMachineToLegacy() converts this to the flat\n * format the dashboard component expects.\n */\nfunction buildProgressState(opts: {\n  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed' | 'cancelled'\n  currentWave: number\n  completedWaves: string[]\n  currentStepName: string\n  currentSubstepId?: string | null\n  singleStepMode?: boolean\n  stepPaused?: boolean\n  pausedAtStep?: string | null\n  mockLLM?: boolean\n  stepsDetail?: Array<{ name: string; status: string; duration?: number }>\n}) {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  return {\n    workflowId: `wf_test_${Date.now()}`,\n    workflowName: 'wave-analysis',\n    status: opts.status,\n    stepPaused: opts.stepPaused ?? false,\n    pausedAtStep: opts.pausedAtStep ?? null,\n    progress: {\n      completedSteps: opts.completedWaves,\n      currentWave: opts.currentWave,\n      totalWaves: 4,\n      currentStepIndex: opts.completedWaves.length,\n      currentStepName: opts.currentStepName,\n      currentSubstepId: opts.currentSubstepId ?? null,\n      startTime: now,\n      lastUpdate: now,\n      elapsedSeconds: 10,\n    },\n    config: {\n      singleStepMode: opts.singleStepMode ?? true,\n      stepIntoSubsteps: true,\n      mockLLM: opts.mockLLM ?? true,\n      mockLLMDelay: 100,\n    },\n    stepsDetail: opts.stepsDetail ?? [],\n  }\n}\n\nfunction writeProgress(state: ReturnType<typeof buildProgressState>) {\n  const dir = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data')\n  if (!existsSync(dir)) mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })\n  writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(state, null, 2))\n}\n\n/**\n * Navigate to UKB tab and wait for workflow graph to render.\n * The dashboard polls /api/ukb/processes every ~2s.\n */\nasync function navigateToWorkflowGraph(page: Page) {\n  await page.goto(DASHBOARD_URL)\n  // Click UKB tab\n  const ukbTab = page.getByRole('tab', { name: /UKB/i }).or(page.locator('text=UKB'))\n  await ukbTab.first().click()\n  // Wait for graph SVG to appear\n  await page.waitForSelector('svg', { timeout: 15_000 })\n  // Wait for the polling to pick up our progress state\n  await page.waitForTimeout(3000)\n}\n\n/**\n * Wait for the dashboard to reflect the current progress file state.\n * Polls until the expected node status appears.\n */\nasync function waitForNodeStatus(page: Page, nodeId: string, expectedStatus: string, timeoutMs = 15_000) {\n  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n    const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status').catch(() => null)\n    if (status === expectedStatus) return\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500)\n  }\n  // Final assertion with proper error message\n  const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n  await expect(node).toHaveAttribute('data-status', expectedStatus, { timeout: 2000 })\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Setup / Teardown\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.beforeAll(async () => {\n  // Save existing progress file\n  if (existsSync(PROGRESS_FILE)) {\n    savedProgress = readFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, 'utf8')\n  }\n})\n\ntest.afterAll(async () => {\n  // Restore previous progress file\n  if (savedProgress !== null) {\n    writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, savedProgress)\n  }\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: \"Data Preparation\" naming (not \"Batch\")\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Workflow Graph Naming', () => {\n  test('batch_scheduler node shows \"Prep\" label, not \"Batch\"', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Set up a simple running workflow so nodes appear\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_init',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_init',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    const label = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-label-batch_scheduler\"]')\n    await expect(label).toBeVisible({ timeout: 15_000 })\n    const text = await label.textContent()\n    expect(text).toBe('Prep')\n    // Make sure \"Batch\" doesn't appear\n    expect(text).not.toContain('Batch')\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Node colors for different states\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Node Colors', () => {\n\n  test('pending nodes have grey fill (#f9fafb)', async ({ page }) => {\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_init',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave1_init',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_init',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Nodes that should be pending: quality_assurance, persistence, insight_generation\n    for (const nodeId of ['quality_assurance', 'persistence', 'insight_generation']) {\n      const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have pending fill`).toBe(COLORS.pending.fill)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('completed nodes have green fill (#166534) and stroke (#15803d)', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave 1 completed, wave 2 running at analyze step\n    // This means batch_scheduler and semantic_analysis (from wave1) should be completed\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // When wave1 is completed, WAVE_AGENTS maps it to:\n    // semantic_analysis, ontology_classification, quality_assurance, persistence, kg_operators\n    // These should all show completed (green)\n    const expectedCompleted = [\n      'semantic_analysis',\n      'ontology_classification',\n      'quality_assurance',\n      'persistence',\n      'kg_operators',\n    ]\n\n    for (const nodeId of expectedCompleted) {\n      const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        const stroke = await rect.getAttribute('stroke')\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have completed fill`).toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n        expect(stroke, `${nodeId} should have completed stroke`).toBe(COLORS.completed.stroke)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('running node has bold strokeWidth 4', async ({ page }) => {\n    // wave1_analyze maps to semantic_analysis which should be \"running\"\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave1_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_analyze',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // batch_scheduler should be completed (before semantic_analysis in WAVE_SUBSTEP_SEQUENCE)\n    await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'batch_scheduler', 'completed')\n    const batchRect = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-rect-batch_scheduler\"]')\n    const batchFill = await batchRect.getAttribute('fill')\n    expect(batchFill, 'batch_scheduler should be green (completed)').toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n    const batchStrokeWidth = await batchRect.getAttribute('stroke-width') ?? await batchRect.getAttribute('strokeWidth')\n    expect(batchStrokeWidth, 'completed strokeWidth should be 2').toBe(COLORS.completed.strokeWidth)\n  })\n\n  test('status indicator circles show correct colors', async ({ page }) => {\n    // wave1 completed, wave2 running\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Completed nodes should have green indicator\n    const completedIndicator = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-status-indicator-semantic_analysis\"]')\n    if (await completedIndicator.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n      const fill = await completedIndicator.getAttribute('fill')\n      expect(fill, 'completed indicator should be green').toBe(COLORS.statusIndicator.completed)\n    }\n\n    // insight_generation should still be pending\n    const pendingIndicator = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-status-indicator-insight_generation\"]')\n    if (await pendingIndicator.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n      const fill = await pendingIndicator.getAttribute('fill')\n      expect(fill, 'pending indicator should be grey').toBe(COLORS.statusIndicator.pending)\n    }\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Sub-step arc colors\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Sub-step Arc Colors', () => {\n\n  test('completed sub-steps show green arcs when agent is completed', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave1 completed — semantic_analysis and its substeps should be green\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Need to expand substeps first by clicking the badge\n    const semNode = page.locator('[data-testid=\"workflow-node-semantic_analysis\"]')\n    await semNode.click()\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500)\n\n    // Check if substep arcs are visible and have correct status\n    const substepIds = ['sem_data_prep', 'sem_llm_analysis', 'sem_observation_gen', 'sem_entity_transform']\n    for (const substepId of substepIds) {\n      const substep = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"substep-semantic_analysis-${substepId}\"]`)\n      if (await substep.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const status = await substep.getAttribute('data-status')\n        expect(status, `substep ${substepId} should be completed`).toBe('completed')\n        const path = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"substep-path-semantic_analysis-${substepId}\"]`)\n        const fill = await path.getAttribute('fill')\n        expect(fill, `substep ${substepId} arc should be green`).toBe(COLORS.substep.completed.fill)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Step advancement state transitions (no jumps)\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Step Advancement', () => {\n\n  test('stepping through wave1 sub-steps follows correct sequence', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Start at wave1_init (batch_scheduler)\n    const wave1Steps = [\n      { step: 'wave1_init',     expectedAgent: 'batch_scheduler',        priorCompleted: [] as string[] },\n      { step: 'wave1_analyze',  expectedAgent: 'semantic_analysis',      priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_qa',       expectedAgent: 'quality_assurance',      priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_classify', expectedAgent: 'ontology_classification', priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_persist',  expectedAgent: 'persistence',           priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance', 'ontology_classification'] },\n    ]\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < wave1Steps.length; i++) {\n      const { step, expectedAgent, priorCompleted } = wave1Steps[i]\n\n      writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n        status: 'running',\n        currentWave: 1,\n        completedWaves: [],\n        currentStepName: step,\n        currentSubstepId: step,\n        singleStepMode: true,\n        stepPaused: true,\n        pausedAtStep: step,\n      }))\n\n      // Wait for dashboard to pick up the new state\n      if (i === 0) {\n        await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n      } else {\n        await page.waitForTimeout(3000) // Poll interval\n      }\n\n      // Verify the expected agent node status\n      await waitForNodeStatus(page, expectedAgent, 'running', 15_000)\n\n      // All prior agents in the sequence should be completed (green)\n      for (const priorAgent of priorCompleted) {\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${priorAgent}\"]`)\n        if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n          expect(fill, `${priorAgent} should be completed (green) when at step ${step}`).toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Agents AFTER the current one should still be pending\n      const allSequence = ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance', 'ontology_classification', 'persistence']\n      const currentIdx = allSequence.indexOf(expectedAgent)\n      for (let j = currentIdx + 1; j < allSequence.length; j++) {\n        const futureAgent = allSequence[j]\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${futureAgent}\"]`)\n        if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n          expect(fill, `${futureAgent} should be pending when at step ${step}`).toBe(COLORS.pending.fill)\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('wave completion turns all wave agents green', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave 1 and 2 completed, wave 3 starting\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 3,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1', 'wave2'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave3_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave3_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave3_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n        { name: 'wave2', status: 'completed', duration: 150 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // All wave agents should be completed from wave1+wave2\n    const waveAgents = ['semantic_analysis', 'ontology_classification', 'quality_assurance', 'persistence', 'kg_operators']\n    for (const nodeId of waveAgents) {\n      const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status')\n        // Should be completed or running (if currentStep maps to it)\n        expect(\n          ['completed', 'running'].includes(status ?? ''),\n          `${nodeId} should be completed or running after wave1+wave2 done, got \"${status}\"`\n        ).toBe(true)\n\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        // Both completed (#166534) and running (#166534) use the same green fill\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have green fill`).toBe('#166534')\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('no state jumps: sequential steps update one node at a time', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Track which nodes change status between steps\n    const statusSnapshots: Record<string, Record<string, string>> = {}\n\n    const steps = [\n      { step: 'wave1_init',    substep: 'wave1_init' },\n      { step: 'wave1_analyze', substep: 'wave1_analyze' },\n      { step: 'wave1_qa',     substep: 'wave1_qa' },\n    ]\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\n      writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n        status: 'running',\n        currentWave: 1,\n        completedWaves: [],\n        currentStepName: steps[i].step,\n        currentSubstepId: steps[i].substep,\n        singleStepMode: true,\n        stepPaused: true,\n        pausedAtStep: steps[i].step,\n      }))\n\n      if (i === 0) {\n        await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n      } else {\n        await page.waitForTimeout(3000)\n      }\n\n      // Capture all node statuses\n      const snapshot: Record<string, string> = {}\n      const allNodes = ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance',\n                        'ontology_classification', 'persistence', 'kg_operators', 'insight_generation']\n      for (const nodeId of allNodes) {\n        const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n        if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status')\n          snapshot[nodeId] = status ?? 'unknown'\n        }\n      }\n      statusSnapshots[steps[i].step] = snapshot\n\n      // After first step, check that transitions are incremental (no jumps)\n      if (i > 0) {\n        const prevStep = steps[i - 1].step\n        const prev = statusSnapshots[prevStep]\n        const curr = snapshot\n\n        // Count how many nodes changed status\n        let changedNodes = 0\n        const changes: string[] = []\n        for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n          if (prev[nodeId] && prev[nodeId] !== curr[nodeId]) {\n            changedNodes++\n            changes.push(`${nodeId}: ${prev[nodeId]} → ${curr[nodeId]}`)\n          }\n        }\n\n        // At most 2 nodes should change per step (the previously running node\n        // becomes completed, and the next node becomes running)\n        expect(\n          changedNodes,\n          `Step ${prevStep} → ${steps[i].step}: too many nodes changed (${changedNodes}): ${changes.join(', ')}`\n        ).toBeLessThanOrEqual(2)\n\n        // No node should jump from pending to completed (skipping running)\n        for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n          if (prev[nodeId] === 'pending' && curr[nodeId] === 'completed') {\n            throw new Error(\n              `State jump detected: ${nodeId} went from pending to completed ` +\n              `(skipping running) between ${prevStep} → ${steps[i].step}`\n            )\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  })\n})\n"
}
```

  "content": "/**\n * Playwright E2E tests for UKB Workflow Graph node coloring.\n * Tests the multi-agent-graph.tsx component (the ACTIVE graph renderer).\n *\n * Validates:\n * 1. Completed steps turn green (data-status=\"completed\")\n * 2. Running steps show running state (data-status=\"running\")\n * 3. Step advancement doesn't cause state jumps\n */\n\nimport { test, expect, type Page } from '@playwright/test'\nimport { writeFileSync, existsSync, readFileSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs'\nimport { join, dirname } from 'path'\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url'\n\nconst __filename2 = fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url)\nconst __dirname2 = dirname(__filename2)\nconst CODING_ROOT = join(__dirname2, '..', '..', '..')\nconst PROGRESS_FILE = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data', 'workflow-progress.json')\n\nfunction buildProgressState(opts: {\n  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed'\n  currentWave: number\n  completedWaves: string[]\n  currentStepName: string\n  currentSubstepId?: string | null\n  stepsDetail?: Array<{ name: string; status: string; duration?: number }>\n}) {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  return {\n    workflowId: `wf_test_${Date.now()}`,\n    workflowName: 'wave-analysis',\n    status: opts.status,\n    stepPaused: true,\n    pausedAtStep: opts.currentStepName,\n    progress: {\n      completedSteps: opts.completedWaves,\n      currentWave: opts.currentWave,\n      totalWaves: 4,\n      currentStepIndex: opts.completedWaves.length,\n      currentStepName: opts.currentStepName,\n      currentSubstepId: opts.currentSubstepId ?? null,\n      startTime: now,\n      lastUpdate: now,\n      elapsedSeconds: 10,\n    },\n    config: {\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepIntoSubsteps: true,\n      mockLLM: true,\n      mockLLMDelay: 100,\n    },\n    stepsDetail: opts.stepsDetail ?? [],\n  }\n}\n\nfunction writeProgress(state: ReturnType<typeof buildProgressState>) {\n  const dir = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data')\n  if (!existsSync(dir)) mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })\n  writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(state, null, 2))\n}\n\nasync function navigateToWorkflowGraph(page: Page) {\n  await page.goto('http://localhost:3032')\n  const ukbTab = page.getByRole('tab', { name: /UKB/i }).or(page.locator('text=UKB'))\n  await ukbTab.first().click()\n  // Wait for graph SVG with data-testid attributes to appear\n  await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^=\"workflow-node-\"]', { timeout: 15_000 })\n  // Extra wait for polling to settle\n  await page.waitForTimeout(2000)\n}\n\nasync function waitForNodeStatus(page: expectedStatus, { timeout: timeoutMs })\n}\n\nlet savedProgress: string | null = null\n\ntest.beforeAll(async () => {\n  if (existsSync(PROGRESS_FILE)) {\n    savedProgress = readFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, 'utf8')\n  }\n})\n\ntest.afterAll(async () => {\n  if (savedProgress !== null) {\n    writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, savedProgress)\n  }\n})\n\n// ── Naming expect(text).not.toContain('Batch')\n})\n\n// ── Node status coloring ──\n\ntest('completed wave marks agent nodes as completed', async ({ page }) => {\n  // Wave 1 completed, wave 2 running at analyze\n  writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n    status: 'running',\n    currentWave: 2,\n    completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n    currentSubstepId: of ['semantic_analysis', 'ontology_classification', 'quality_assurance', 'persistence']) {\n    await waitForNodeStatus(page, nodeId, 'completed')\n  }\n})\n\ntest('currently running step maps to currentSubstepId: 'wave1_analyze',\n  }))\n  await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n  await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'semantic_analysis', 'running')\n})\n\ntest('prior agents in wave sequence are for (const nodeId of allNodes) {\n      const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        snapshot[nodeId] = await node.getAttribute('data-status') ?? 'unknown'\n      }\n    }\n    snapshots[steps[i].step] = snapshot\n\n    // Check no state jumps from previous step\n    if (i > 0) {\n      const prev = snapshots[steps[i - 1].step]\n      const curr = snapshot\n      for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n        if (prev[nodeId] === 'pending' && curr[nodeId] === 'completed') {\n          throw new Error(\n            `State jump: ${nodeId} went pending→completed (skipping running) ` +\n            `between ${steps[i - 1].step}→${steps[i].step}`\n          )\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n})\n"

{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>dashboard/workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * Playwright E2E tests for UKB Workflow Graph node coloring.\n *\n * Validates that:\n * 1. Completed steps turn green (fill #166534, stroke #15803d)\n * 2. Sub-step arcs show correct colors\n * 5. \"Data Preparation\" label appears (not \"Batch\")\n * 6. Step advancement doesn't cause state jumps\n *\n * These tests write workflow-progress.json directly and let the dashboard\n * poll it via its /api/ukb/processes endpoint.\n */\n\nimport { test, expect, type Page } from '@playwright/test'\nimport { writeFileSync, existsSync, readFileSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs'\nimport { join } from 'path'\n\nconst CODING_ROOT = join(__dirname, '..', '..', '..')\nconst PROGRESS_FILE = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data', 'workflow-progress.json')\nconst DASHBOARD_URL = 'http://localhost:3032'\n\n// Expected color constants from ukb-workflow-graph.tsx\nconst COLORS = {\n  completed: { fill: '#166534', stroke: '#15803d', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  running:   { fill: '#166534', stroke: '#22c55e', strokeWidth: '4' },\n  paused:    { fill: '#92400e', stroke: '#f59e0b', strokeWidth: '4' },\n  pending:   { fill: '#f9fafb', stroke: '#d1d5db', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  failed:    { fill: '#fee2e2', stroke: '#ef4444', strokeWidth: '2' },\n  // Status indicator circle colors\n  statusIndicator: {\n    completed: '#22c55e',\n    running: '#3b82f6',\n    failed: '#ef4444',\n    pending: '#d1d5db',\n  },\n  // Sub-step arc colors\n  substep: {\n    completed: { fill: '#22c55e', stroke: '#16a34a' },\n    running:   { fill: '#3b82f6', stroke: '#2563eb' },\n    pending:   { fill: '#e5e7eb', stroke: '#9ca3af' },\n  },\n}\n\n// Saved progress to restore after tests\nlet savedProgress: string | null = null\n\n/**\n * Build a state-machine-format workflow-progress.json.\n * The server.js bridgeStateMachineToLegacy() converts this to the flat\n * format the dashboard component expects.\n */\nfunction buildProgressState(opts: {\n  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed' | 'cancelled'\n  currentWave: number\n  completedWaves: string[]\n  currentStepName: string\n  currentSubstepId?: string | null\n  singleStepMode?: boolean\n  stepPaused?: boolean\n  pausedAtStep?: string | null\n  mockLLM?: boolean\n  stepsDetail?: Array<{ name: string; status: string; duration?: number }>\n}) {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  return {\n    workflowId: `wf_test_${Date.now()}`,\n    workflowName: 'wave-analysis',\n    status: opts.status,\n    stepPaused: opts.stepPaused ?? false,\n    pausedAtStep: opts.pausedAtStep ?? null,\n    progress: {\n      completedSteps: opts.completedWaves,\n      currentWave: opts.currentWave,\n      totalWaves: 4,\n      currentStepIndex: opts.completedWaves.length,\n      currentStepName: opts.currentStepName,\n      currentSubstepId: opts.currentSubstepId ?? null,\n      startTime: now,\n      lastUpdate: now,\n      elapsedSeconds: 10,\n    },\n    config: {\n      singleStepMode: opts.singleStepMode ?? true,\n      stepIntoSubsteps: true,\n      mockLLM: opts.mockLLM ?? true,\n      mockLLMDelay: 100,\n    },\n    stepsDetail: opts.stepsDetail ?? [],\n  }\n}\n\nfunction writeProgress(state: ReturnType<typeof buildProgressState>) {\n  const dir = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data')\n  if (!existsSync(dir)) mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })\n  writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(state, null, 2))\n}\n\n/**\n * Navigate to UKB tab and wait for workflow graph to render.\n * The dashboard polls /api/ukb/processes every ~2s.\n */\nasync function navigateToWorkflowGraph(page: Page) {\n  await page.goto(DASHBOARD_URL)\n  // Click UKB tab\n  const ukbTab = page.getByRole('tab', { name: /UKB/i }).or(page.locator('text=UKB'))\n  await ukbTab.first().click()\n  // Wait for graph SVG to appear\n  await page.waitForSelector('svg', { timeout: 15_000 })\n  // Wait for the polling to pick up our progress state\n  await page.waitForTimeout(3000)\n}\n\n/**\n * Wait for the dashboard to reflect the current progress file state.\n * Polls until the expected node status appears.\n */\nasync function waitForNodeStatus(page: Page, nodeId: string, expectedStatus: string, timeoutMs = 15_000) {\n  const deadline = Date.now() + timeoutMs\n  while (Date.now() < deadline) {\n    const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n    const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status').catch(() => null)\n    if (status === expectedStatus) return\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500)\n  }\n  // Final assertion with proper error message\n  const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n  await expect(node).toHaveAttribute('data-status', expectedStatus, { timeout: 2000 })\n}\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Setup / Teardown\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.beforeAll(async () => {\n  // Save existing progress file\n  if (existsSync(PROGRESS_FILE)) {\n    savedProgress = readFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, 'utf8')\n  }\n})\n\ntest.afterAll(async () => {\n  // Restore previous progress file\n  if (savedProgress !== null) {\n    writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, savedProgress)\n  }\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: \"Data Preparation\" naming (not \"Batch\")\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Workflow Graph Naming', () => {\n  test('batch_scheduler node shows \"Prep\" label, not \"Batch\"', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Set up a simple running workflow so nodes appear\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_init',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_init',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    const label = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-label-batch_scheduler\"]')\n    await expect(label).toBeVisible({ timeout: 15_000 })\n    const text = await label.textContent()\n    expect(text).toBe('Prep')\n    // Make sure \"Batch\" doesn't appear\n    expect(text).not.toContain('Batch')\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Node colors for different states\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Node Colors', () => {\n\n  test('pending nodes have grey fill (#f9fafb)', async ({ page }) => {\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_init',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave1_init',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_init',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Nodes that should be pending: quality_assurance, persistence, insight_generation\n    for (const nodeId of ['quality_assurance', 'persistence', 'insight_generation']) {\n      const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have pending fill`).toBe(COLORS.pending.fill)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('completed nodes have green fill (#166534) and stroke (#15803d)', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave 1 completed, wave 2 running at analyze step\n    // This means batch_scheduler and semantic_analysis (from wave1) should be completed\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // When wave1 is completed, WAVE_AGENTS maps it to:\n    // semantic_analysis, ontology_classification, quality_assurance, persistence, kg_operators\n    // These should all show completed (green)\n    const expectedCompleted = [\n      'semantic_analysis',\n      'ontology_classification',\n      'quality_assurance',\n      'persistence',\n      'kg_operators',\n    ]\n\n    for (const nodeId of expectedCompleted) {\n      const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        const stroke = await rect.getAttribute('stroke')\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have completed fill`).toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n        expect(stroke, `${nodeId} should have completed stroke`).toBe(COLORS.completed.stroke)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('running node has bold strokeWidth 4', async ({ page }) => {\n    // wave1_analyze maps to semantic_analysis which should be \"running\"\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: 'wave1_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave1_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave1_analyze',\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // batch_scheduler should be completed (before semantic_analysis in WAVE_SUBSTEP_SEQUENCE)\n    await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'batch_scheduler', 'completed')\n    const batchRect = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-rect-batch_scheduler\"]')\n    const batchFill = await batchRect.getAttribute('fill')\n    expect(batchFill, 'batch_scheduler should be green (completed)').toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n    const batchStrokeWidth = await batchRect.getAttribute('stroke-width') ?? await batchRect.getAttribute('strokeWidth')\n    expect(batchStrokeWidth, 'completed strokeWidth should be 2').toBe(COLORS.completed.strokeWidth)\n  })\n\n  test('status indicator circles show correct colors', async ({ page }) => {\n    // wave1 completed, wave2 running\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Completed nodes should have green indicator\n    const completedIndicator = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-status-indicator-semantic_analysis\"]')\n    if (await completedIndicator.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n      const fill = await completedIndicator.getAttribute('fill')\n      expect(fill, 'completed indicator should be green').toBe(COLORS.statusIndicator.completed)\n    }\n\n    // insight_generation should still be pending\n    const pendingIndicator = page.locator('[data-testid=\"node-status-indicator-insight_generation\"]')\n    if (await pendingIndicator.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n      const fill = await pendingIndicator.getAttribute('fill')\n      expect(fill, 'pending indicator should be grey').toBe(COLORS.statusIndicator.pending)\n    }\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Sub-step arc colors\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Sub-step Arc Colors', () => {\n\n  test('completed sub-steps show green arcs when agent is completed', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave1 completed — semantic_analysis and its substeps should be green\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 2,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave2_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // Need to expand substeps first by clicking the badge\n    const semNode = page.locator('[data-testid=\"workflow-node-semantic_analysis\"]')\n    await semNode.click()\n    await page.waitForTimeout(500)\n\n    // Check if substep arcs are visible and have correct status\n    const substepIds = ['sem_data_prep', 'sem_llm_analysis', 'sem_observation_gen', 'sem_entity_transform']\n    for (const substepId of substepIds) {\n      const substep = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"substep-semantic_analysis-${substepId}\"]`)\n      if (await substep.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const status = await substep.getAttribute('data-status')\n        expect(status, `substep ${substepId} should be completed`).toBe('completed')\n        const path = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"substep-path-semantic_analysis-${substepId}\"]`)\n        const fill = await path.getAttribute('fill')\n        expect(fill, `substep ${substepId} arc should be green`).toBe(COLORS.substep.completed.fill)\n      }\n    }\n  })\n})\n\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n// Test: Step advancement state transitions (no jumps)\n// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\ntest.describe('Step Advancement', () => {\n\n  test('stepping through wave1 sub-steps follows correct sequence', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Start at wave1_init (batch_scheduler)\n    const wave1Steps = [\n      { step: 'wave1_init',     expectedAgent: 'batch_scheduler',        priorCompleted: [] as string[] },\n      { step: 'wave1_analyze',  expectedAgent: 'semantic_analysis',      priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_qa',       expectedAgent: 'quality_assurance',      priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_classify', expectedAgent: 'ontology_classification', priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance'] },\n      { step: 'wave1_persist',  expectedAgent: 'persistence',           priorCompleted: ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance', 'ontology_classification'] },\n    ]\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < wave1Steps.length; i++) {\n      const { step, expectedAgent, priorCompleted } = wave1Steps[i]\n\n      writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n        status: 'running',\n        currentWave: 1,\n        completedWaves: [],\n        currentStepName: step,\n        currentSubstepId: step,\n        singleStepMode: true,\n        stepPaused: true,\n        pausedAtStep: step,\n      }))\n\n      // Wait for dashboard to pick up the new state\n      if (i === 0) {\n        await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n      } else {\n        await page.waitForTimeout(3000) // Poll interval\n      }\n\n      // Verify the expected agent node status\n      await waitForNodeStatus(page, expectedAgent, 'running', 15_000)\n\n      // All prior agents in the sequence should be completed (green)\n      for (const priorAgent of priorCompleted) {\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${priorAgent}\"]`)\n        if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n          expect(fill, `${priorAgent} should be completed (green) when at step ${step}`).toBe(COLORS.completed.fill)\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Agents AFTER the current one should still be pending\n      const allSequence = ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance', 'ontology_classification', 'persistence']\n      const currentIdx = allSequence.indexOf(expectedAgent)\n      for (let j = currentIdx + 1; j < allSequence.length; j++) {\n        const futureAgent = allSequence[j]\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${futureAgent}\"]`)\n        if (await rect.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n          expect(fill, `${futureAgent} should be pending when at step ${step}`).toBe(COLORS.pending.fill)\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('wave completion turns all wave agents green', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Wave 1 and 2 completed, wave 3 starting\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 3,\n      completedWaves: ['wave1', 'wave2'],\n      currentStepName: 'wave3_analyze',\n      currentSubstepId: 'wave3_analyze',\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepPaused: true,\n      pausedAtStep: 'wave3_analyze',\n      stepsDetail: [\n        { name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 },\n        { name: 'wave2', status: 'completed', duration: 150 },\n      ],\n    }))\n\n    await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n    // All wave agents should be completed from wave1+wave2\n    const waveAgents = ['semantic_analysis', 'ontology_classification', 'quality_assurance', 'persistence', 'kg_operators']\n    for (const nodeId of waveAgents) {\n      const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status')\n        // Should be completed or running (if currentStep maps to it)\n        expect(\n          ['completed', 'running'].includes(status ?? ''),\n          `${nodeId} should be completed or running after wave1+wave2 done, got \"${status}\"`\n        ).toBe(true)\n\n        const rect = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"node-rect-${nodeId}\"]`)\n        const fill = await rect.getAttribute('fill')\n        // Both completed (#166534) and running (#166534) use the same green fill\n        expect(fill, `${nodeId} should have green fill`).toBe('#166534')\n      }\n    }\n  })\n\n  test('no state jumps: sequential steps update one node at a time', async ({ page }) => {\n    // Track which nodes change status between steps\n    const statusSnapshots: Record<string, Record<string, string>> = {}\n\n    const steps = [\n      { step: 'wave1_init',    substep: 'wave1_init' },\n      { step: 'wave1_analyze', substep: 'wave1_analyze' },\n      { step: 'wave1_qa',     substep: 'wave1_qa' },\n    ]\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\n      writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n        status: 'running',\n        currentWave: 1,\n        completedWaves: [],\n        currentStepName: steps[i].step,\n        currentSubstepId: steps[i].substep,\n        singleStepMode: true,\n        stepPaused: true,\n        pausedAtStep: steps[i].step,\n      }))\n\n      if (i === 0) {\n        await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n      } else {\n        await page.waitForTimeout(3000)\n      }\n\n      // Capture all node statuses\n      const snapshot: Record<string, string> = {}\n      const allNodes = ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance',\n                        'ontology_classification', 'persistence', 'kg_operators', 'insight_generation']\n      for (const nodeId of allNodes) {\n        const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n        if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n          const status = await node.getAttribute('data-status')\n          snapshot[nodeId] = status ?? 'unknown'\n        }\n      }\n      statusSnapshots[steps[i].step] = snapshot\n\n      // After first step, check that transitions are incremental (no jumps)\n      if (i > 0) {\n        const prevStep = steps[i - 1].step\n        const prev = statusSnapshots[prevStep]\n        const curr = snapshot\n\n        // Count how many nodes changed status\n        let changedNodes = 0\n        const changes: string[] = []\n        for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n          if (prev[nodeId] && prev[nodeId] !== curr[nodeId]) {\n            changedNodes++\n            changes.push(`${nodeId}: ${prev[nodeId]} → ${curr[nodeId]}`)\n          }\n        }\n\n        // At most 2 nodes should change per step (the previously running node\n        // becomes completed, and the next node becomes running)\n        expect(\n          changedNodes,\n          `Step ${prevStep} → ${steps[i].step}: too many nodes changed (${changedNodes}): ${changes.join(', ')}`\n        ).toBeLessThanOrEqual(2)\n\n        // No node should jump from pending to completed (skipping running)\n        for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n          if (prev[nodeId] === 'pending' && curr[nodeId] === 'completed') {\n            throw new Error(\n              `State jump detected: ${nodeId} went from pending to completed ` +\n              `(skipping running) between ${prevStep} → ${steps[i].step}`\n            )\n          }\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  })\n})\n"
}
```

**Input:** ```json
{
  "file_path": "<AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>dashboard/workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * Playwright E2E tests for UKB Workflow Graph node coloring.\n * Tests the multi-agent-graph.tsx component (the ACTIVE graph renderer).\n *\n * Validates:\n * 1. Completed steps turn green (data-status=\"completed\")\n * 2. Running steps show running state (data-status=\"running\")\n * 3. Pending steps stay pending (data-status=\"pending\")\n * 4. \"Prep\" label appears (not \"Batch\") after YAML rename\n * 5. Step advancement doesn't cause state jumps\n */\n\nimport { test, expect, type Page } from '@playwright/test'\nimport { writeFileSync, existsSync, readFileSync, mkdirSync } from 'fs'\nimport { join, dirname } from 'path'\nimport { fileURLToPath } from 'url'\n\nconst __filename2 = fileURLToPath(import.<COMPANY_NAME_REDACTED>.url)\nconst __dirname2 = dirname(__filename2)\nconst CODING_ROOT = join(__dirname2, '..', '..', '..')\nconst PROGRESS_FILE = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data', 'workflow-progress.json')\n\nfunction buildProgressState(opts: {\n  status: 'running' | 'paused' | 'completed'\n  currentWave: number\n  completedWaves: string[]\n  currentStepName: string\n  currentSubstepId?: string | null\n  stepsDetail?: Array<{ name: string; status: string; duration?: number }>\n}) {\n  const now = new Date().toISOString()\n  return {\n    workflowId: `wf_test_${Date.now()}`,\n    workflowName: 'wave-analysis',\n    status: opts.status,\n    stepPaused: true,\n    pausedAtStep: opts.currentStepName,\n    progress: {\n      completedSteps: opts.completedWaves,\n      currentWave: opts.currentWave,\n      totalWaves: 4,\n      currentStepIndex: opts.completedWaves.length,\n      currentStepName: opts.currentStepName,\n      currentSubstepId: opts.currentSubstepId ?? null,\n      startTime: now,\n      lastUpdate: now,\n      elapsedSeconds: 10,\n    },\n    config: {\n      singleStepMode: true,\n      stepIntoSubsteps: true,\n      mockLLM: true,\n      mockLLMDelay: 100,\n    },\n    stepsDetail: opts.stepsDetail ?? [],\n  }\n}\n\nfunction writeProgress(state: ReturnType<typeof buildProgressState>) {\n  const dir = join(CODING_ROOT, '.data')\n  if (!existsSync(dir)) mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true })\n  writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, JSON.stringify(state, null, 2))\n}\n\nasync function navigateToWorkflowGraph(page: Page) {\n  await page.goto('http://localhost:3032')\n  const ukbTab = page.getByRole('tab', { name: /UKB/i }).or(page.locator('text=UKB'))\n  await ukbTab.first().click()\n  // Wait for graph SVG with data-testid attributes to appear\n  await page.waitForSelector('[data-testid^=\"workflow-node-\"]', { timeout: 15_000 })\n  // Extra wait for polling to settle\n  await page.waitForTimeout(2000)\n}\n\nasync function waitForNodeStatus(page: Page, nodeId: string, expectedStatus: string, timeoutMs = 15_000) {\n  const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n  await expect(node).toHaveAttribute('data-status', expectedStatus, { timeout: timeoutMs })\n}\n\nlet savedProgress: string | null = null\n\ntest.beforeAll(async () => {\n  if (existsSync(PROGRESS_FILE)) {\n    savedProgress = readFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, 'utf8')\n  }\n})\n\ntest.afterAll(async () => {\n  if (savedProgress !== null) {\n    writeFileSync(PROGRESS_FILE, savedProgress)\n  }\n})\n\n// ── Naming ──\n\ntest('batch_scheduler node shows \"Prep\" label, not \"Batch\"', async ({ page }) => {\n  writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n    status: 'running',\n    currentWave: 1,\n    completedWaves: [],\n    currentStepName: 'wave1_init',\n  }))\n  await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n  // The graph text comes from YAML via API — check the node's text content\n  const node = page.locator('[data-testid=\"workflow-node-batch_scheduler\"]')\n  await expect(node).toBeVisible({ timeout: 15_000 })\n  const text = await node.textContent()\n  expect(text).toContain('Prep')\n  expect(text).not.toContain('Batch')\n})\n\n// ── Node status coloring ──\n\ntest('completed wave marks agent nodes as completed', async ({ page }) => {\n  // Wave 1 completed, wave 2 running at analyze\n  writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n    status: 'running',\n    currentWave: 2,\n    completedWaves: ['wave1'],\n    currentStepName: 'wave2_analyze',\n    currentSubstepId: 'wave2_analyze',\n    stepsDetail: [{ name: 'wave1', status: 'completed', duration: 120 }],\n  }))\n  await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n\n  // Wave1 agents should be completed\n  for (const nodeId of ['semantic_analysis', 'ontology_classification', 'quality_assurance', 'persistence']) {\n    await waitForNodeStatus(page, nodeId, 'completed')\n  }\n})\n\ntest('currently running step maps to running agent node', async ({ page }) => {\n  writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n    status: 'running',\n    currentWave: 1,\n    completedWaves: [],\n    currentStepName: 'wave1_analyze',\n    currentSubstepId: 'wave1_analyze',\n  }))\n  await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n  await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'semantic_analysis', 'running')\n})\n\ntest('prior agents in wave sequence are completed when later step runs', async ({ page }) => {\n  // At wave1_analyze, batch_scheduler should be completed\n  writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n    status: 'running',\n    currentWave: 1,\n    completedWaves: [],\n    currentStepName: 'wave1_analyze',\n  }))\n  await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n  await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'batch_scheduler', 'completed')\n  await waitForNodeStatus(page, 'semantic_analysis', 'running')\n})\n\n// ── Step advancement: no state jumps ──\n\ntest('sequential steps update one node at a time (no jumps)', async ({ page }) => {\n  const steps = [\n    { step: 'wave1_init',    agent: 'batch_scheduler' },\n    { step: 'wave1_analyze', agent: 'semantic_analysis' },\n    { step: 'wave1_qa',      agent: 'quality_assurance' },\n  ]\n  const snapshots: Record<string, Record<string, string>> = {}\n  const allNodes = ['batch_scheduler', 'semantic_analysis', 'quality_assurance',\n                    'ontology_classification', 'persistence', 'kg_operators', 'insight_generation']\n\n  for (let i = 0; i < steps.length; i++) {\n    writeProgress(buildProgressState({\n      status: 'running',\n      currentWave: 1,\n      completedWaves: [],\n      currentStepName: steps[i].step,\n      currentSubstepId: steps[i].step,\n    }))\n\n    if (i === 0) {\n      await navigateToWorkflowGraph(page)\n    } else {\n      await page.waitForTimeout(3500) // Wait for polling\n    }\n\n    await waitForNodeStatus(page, steps[i].agent, 'running')\n\n    // Capture snapshot\n    const snapshot: Record<string, string> = {}\n    for (const nodeId of allNodes) {\n      const node = page.locator(`[data-testid=\"workflow-node-${nodeId}\"]`)\n      if (await node.isVisible().catch(() => false)) {\n        snapshot[nodeId] = await node.getAttribute('data-status') ?? 'unknown'\n      }\n    }\n    snapshots[steps[i].step] = snapshot\n\n    // Check no state jumps from previous step\n    if (i > 0) {\n      const prev = snapshots[steps[i - 1].step]\n      const curr = snapshot\n      for (const nodeId of Object.keys(curr)) {\n        if (prev[nodeId] === 'pending' && curr[nodeId] === 'completed') {\n          throw new Error(\n            `State jump: ${nodeId} went pending→completed (skipping running) ` +\n            `between ${steps[i - 1].step}→${steps[i].step}`\n          )\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n})\n"
}
```

**Output:** ```
The file <AWS_SECRET_REDACTED>dashboard/workflow-graph-colors.spec.ts has been updated successfully.
